58   def run(limit: Int,
59           includeExtraEdges: Boolean,
60           submittedQueryGraph: TRAPIQueryGraph): RIO[ZConfig[AppConfig] with HttpClient with Has[BiolinkData] with Has[SPARQLCache], TRAPIMessage] =
61     for {
62       biolinkData <- biolinkData
63       _ = logger.debug("limit: {}, includeExtraEdges: {}", limit, includeExtraEdges)
64       queryGraph = enforceQueryEdgeTypes(submittedQueryGraph, biolinkData.predicates)
65       allPredicatesInQuery = queryGraph.edges.values.flatMap(_.predicates.getOrElse(Nil)).to(Set)
66       predicatesToRelations <- mapQueryBiolinkPredicatesToRelations(allPredicatesInQuery)
67       allRelationsInQuery = predicatesToRelations.values.flatten.to(Set)
68       relationsToLabelAndBiolinkPredicate <- mapRelationsToLabelAndBiolink(allRelationsInQuery)
69       initialQuerySolutions <- findInitialQuerySolutions(queryGraph, predicatesToRelations, limit)
70       solutionTriples = extractCoreTriples(initialQuerySolutions, queryGraph)
71       provs <- getProvenance(solutionTriples)
72       initialKGNodes <- getTRAPINodes(queryGraph, initialQuerySolutions, biolinkData.classes)
73       initialKGEdges <- getTRAPIEdges(queryGraph, initialQuerySolutions, relationsToLabelAndBiolinkPredicate, provs)
74       querySolutionsToEdgeBindings <- getTRAPIEdgeBindingsMany(queryGraph, initialQuerySolutions, relationsToLabelAndBiolinkPredicate)
75       trapiBindings <- ZIO.foreach(initialQuerySolutions) { querySolution =>
76         getTRAPINodeBindings(queryGraph, querySolution) zip Task.effect(querySolutionsToEdgeBindings(querySolution))
77       }
78       _ <- ZIO.when(includeExtraEdges)(
79         for {
80           prov2CAMStuffTripleMap <- ZIO.foreachPar(provs.values)(prov => getCAMStuff(IRI(prov)).map(prov -> _)).map(_.toMap)
81           allCAMTriples = prov2CAMStuffTripleMap.values.to(Set).flatten
82           allTripleNodes = allCAMTriples.flatMap(t => Set(t.subj, t.obj))
83           slotStuffNodeDetails <- getTRAPINodeDetails(allTripleNodes.to(List))
84           extraKGNodes = getExtraKGNodes(allTripleNodes, slotStuffNodeDetails, biolinkData)
85           allPredicates = allCAMTriples.map(_.pred)
86           relationsToInfo <- mapRelationsToLabelAndBiolink(allPredicates)
87           extraKGEdges = allCAMTriples.flatMap { triple =>
88             for {
89               (relationLabelOpt, relationBiolinkPredicate) <- relationsToInfo.get(triple.pred)
90               predBLTermOpt = biolinkData.predicates.find(a => a.iri == relationBiolinkPredicate)
91               key = getTRAPIEdgeKey(triple.subj.value, predBLTermOpt, triple.obj.value)
92               edge = TRAPIEdge(predBLTermOpt, triple.subj, triple.obj, None)
93             } yield key -> edge
94           }.toMap
95           _ = initialKGNodes ++ extraKGNodes
96           _ = initialKGEdges ++ extraKGEdges
97         } yield ()
98       )
99       results = trapiBindings.map { case (resultNodeBindings, resultEdgeBindings) => TRAPIResult(resultNodeBindings, resultEdgeBindings) }
100     } yield TRAPIMessage(Some(queryGraph), Some(TRAPIKnowledgeGraph(initialKGNodes, initialKGEdges)), Some(results.distinct))
101 
102   def findInitialQuerySolutions(queryGraph: TRAPIQueryGraph,
103                                 predicatesToRelations: Map[BiolinkPredicate, Set[IRI]],
104                                 limit: Int): ZIO[ZConfig[AppConfig] with HttpClient, Throwable, List[QuerySolution]] = {
105     val queryEdgeSparql = queryGraph.edges.map { case (queryEdgeID, queryEdge) =>
106       val relationsForEdge = queryEdge.predicates.getOrElse(Nil).flatMap(predicatesToRelations.getOrElse(_, Set.empty)).to(Set)
107       val predicatesQueryText = relationsForEdge.asSPARQLList
108       val edgeIDVar = Var(queryEdgeID)
109       val edgeSourceVar = Var(queryEdge.subject)
110       val edgeTargetVar = Var(queryEdge.`object`)
111       val predicatesValuesClause = sparql""" FILTER( $edgeIDVar IN ( $predicatesQueryText ) )"""
112       val subjectNode = queryGraph.nodes(queryEdge.subject)
113       val subjectNodeValuesClauses = getNodeValuesClauses(subjectNode.ids, subjectNode.categories, edgeSourceVar)
114       val objectNode = queryGraph.nodes(queryEdge.`object`)
115       val objectNodeValuesClauses = getNodeValuesClauses(objectNode.ids, objectNode.categories, edgeTargetVar)
116       val nodesValuesClauses = List(subjectNodeValuesClauses, objectNodeValuesClauses).fold(sparql"")(_ + _)
117       sparql"""
118               $predicatesValuesClause
119               $nodesValuesClauses
120               $edgeSourceVar $edgeIDVar $edgeTargetVar .
121             """
122     }
123     val projections = getProjections(queryGraph)
124     val nodesToDirectTypes = getNodesToDirectTypes(queryGraph.nodes.keySet)
125     val edgePatterns = queryEdgeSparql.fold(sparql"")(_ + _)
126     val limitSparql = if (limit > 0) sparql" LIMIT $limit" else sparql""
127     val queryString =
128       sparql"""SELECT DISTINCT $projections
129           WHERE {
130             $nodesToDirectTypes
131             $edgePatterns
132           }
133           $limitSparql
134           """
135     SPARQLQueryExecutor.runSelectQuery(queryString.toQuery)
136   }
137 
138   def getNodeValuesClauses(ids: Option[List[IRI]], categories: Option[List[BiolinkClass]], edgeVar: Var): QueryText = (ids, categories) match {
139     case (Some(idsList), _) =>
140       sparql""" VALUES ${edgeVar}_class { ${idsList.asValues} }
141                       $edgeVar $RDFType ${edgeVar}_class .
142                       """
143     case (None, Some(biolinkTypes)) =>
144       val irisList = biolinkTypes.map(_.iri)
145       sparql""" VALUES ${edgeVar}_class { ${irisList.asValues} }
146                       $edgeVar $RDFType ${edgeVar}_class .
147                       """
148     case (None, None) => sparql""
149   }
150 
151   def extractCoreTriples(solutions: List[QuerySolution], queryGraph: TRAPIQueryGraph): Set[Triple] =
152     (for {
153       (queryEdgeID, queryEdge) <- queryGraph.edges
154       solution <- solutions
155     } yield Triple(
156       IRI(solution.getResource(queryEdge.subject).getURI),
157       IRI(solution.getResource(queryEdgeID).getURI),
158       IRI(solution.getResource(queryEdge.`object`).getURI)
159     )).to(Set)
160 
161   def getNodesToDirectTypes(nodeIDs: Set[String]): QueryText =
162     nodeIDs
163       .map { nodeID =>
164         val nodeVar = Var(nodeID)
165         val nodeTypeVar = Var(s"${nodeID}_type")
166         val nodeClassVar = Var(s"${nodeID}_class")
167         sparql""" $nodeVar $SesameDirectType $nodeTypeVar .
168                   $nodeTypeVar $RDFSSubClassOf $nodeClassVar .
169               """
170       }
171       .fold(sparql"")(_ + _)

173 
174   def getProjections(queryGraph: TRAPIQueryGraph): QueryText = {
175     val projectionVariableNames =
176       queryGraph.edges.keys ++
177         queryGraph.edges.flatMap(e => List(e._2.subject, e._2.`object`)) ++
178         queryGraph.nodes.keys.map(queryNodeID => s"${queryNodeID}_type")
179     projectionVariableNames.map(Var(_)).map(v => sparql" $v ").fold(sparql"")(_ + _)
180   }
181 
182   def enforceQueryEdgeTypes(queryGraph: TRAPIQueryGraph, biolinkPredicates: List[BiolinkPredicate]): TRAPIQueryGraph = {
183     val improvedEdgeMap = queryGraph.edges.map { case (edgeID, edge) =>
184       val newPredicates = edge.predicates match {
185         case None       => Some(List(BiolinkPredicate("related_to")))
186         case Some(Nil)  => Some(List(BiolinkPredicate("related_to")))
187         case predicates => predicates
188       }
189       val filteredPredicates = newPredicates.map(_.filter(pred => biolinkPredicates.contains(pred)))
190       edgeID -> edge.copy(predicates = filteredPredicates)
191     }
192     val improvedNodeMap = queryGraph.nodes.map { case (nodeID, node) =>
193       val newCategories = node.categories match {
194         case None       => Some(List(BiolinkNamedThing))
195         case Some(Nil)  => Some(List(BiolinkNamedThing))
196         case categories => categories
197       }
198       nodeID -> node.copy(categories = newCategories)
199     }
200     queryGraph.copy(edges = improvedEdgeMap, nodes = improvedNodeMap)
201   }
202 
203   def getTRAPIEdgeKey(sub: String, pred: Option[BiolinkPredicate], obj: String): String = {
204     val edgeKey = TRAPIEdgeKey(sub, pred, obj).asJson.deepDropNullValues.noSpaces
205     String.format("%064x", new BigInteger(1, messageDigest.digest(edgeKey.getBytes(StandardCharsets.UTF_8))))
206   }
207 
208   def getTRAPIEdges(queryGraph: TRAPIQueryGraph,
209                     querySolutions: List[QuerySolution],
210                     relationsMap: Map[IRI, (Option[String], IRI)],
211                     provs: Map[TripleString, String]): ZIO[ZConfig[AppConfig] with Has[BiolinkData], Throwable, Map[String, TRAPIEdge]] =
212 
213     for {
214       biolinkData <- biolinkData
215       appConfig <- getConfig[AppConfig]
216       trapiEdges <- ZIO.foreach(querySolutions) { querySolution =>
217         for {
218           nodeTypeMap <- Task.effect(queryGraph.nodes.map(entry => (entry._1, IRI(querySolution.getResource(s"${entry._1}_type").getURI))))
219           edges <- ZIO.foreach(queryGraph.edges) { (queryEdgeID, queryEdge) =>
220             for {
221               sourceType <- ZIO.fromOption(nodeTypeMap.get(queryEdge.subject)).orElseFail(new Exception("could not get source id"))
222               targetType <- ZIO.fromOption(nodeTypeMap.get(queryEdge.`object`)).orElseFail(new Exception("could not get target id"))
223               source = querySolution.getResource(queryEdge.subject).getURI
224               target = querySolution.getResource(queryEdge.`object`).getURI
225               predicate = querySolution.getResource(queryEdgeID).getURI
226               predicateIRI = IRI(predicate)
227               tripleString = TripleString(source, predicate, target)
228               originalKS <- ZIO.fromOption(biolinkData.predicates.find(p => p.shorthand == "original_knowledge_source")).orElseFail(new Exception("could not get biolink:original_knowledge_source"))
229               aggregatorKS <- ZIO.fromOption(biolinkData.predicates.find(p => p.shorthand == "aggregator_knowledge_source")).orElseFail(new Exception("could not get biolink:aggregator_knowledge_source"))
230               provValue <- ZIO.fromOption(provs.get(tripleString)).orElseFail(new Exception("no prov value"))
231               infoResBiolinkClass <- ZIO.fromOption(biolinkData.classes.find(p => p.shorthand == "InformationResource")).orElseFail(new Exception("could not get biolink:InformationResource"))
232               aggregatorKSAttribute = TRAPIAttribute(Some("infores:cam-kp"), aggregatorKS.iri, None, List("infores:cam-kp"), Some(infoResBiolinkClass.iri), Some(appConfig.location), None, None)
233               originalKSAttribute = TRAPIAttribute(Some("infores:cam-kp"), originalKS.iri, None, List("infores:go-cam"), Some(infoResBiolinkClass.iri), Some(provValue), None, None)
234               attributes = List(aggregatorKSAttribute, originalKSAttribute)
235               relationLabelAndBiolinkPredicate <- ZIO
236                 .fromOption(relationsMap.get(predicateIRI))
237                 .orElseFail(new Exception("Unexpected edge relation"))
238               (relationLabelOpt, biolinkPredicateIRI) = relationLabelAndBiolinkPredicate
239               blPred = biolinkData.predicates.find(a => a.iri == biolinkPredicateIRI)
240               trapiEdgeKey = getTRAPIEdgeKey(sourceType.value, blPred, targetType.value)
241               //FIXME add relation CURIE here?
242               trapiEdge = TRAPIEdge(blPred, sourceType, targetType, Some(attributes))
243             } yield trapiEdgeKey -> trapiEdge
244           }
245         } yield edges.toList
246       }
247     } yield trapiEdges.flatten.toMap
248 
249   def getTRAPINodes(queryGraph: TRAPIQueryGraph, querySolutions: List[QuerySolution], bionlinkClasses: List[BiolinkClass])
250     : RIO[ZConfig[AppConfig] with HttpClient with Has[BiolinkData], Map[IRI, TRAPINode]] = {
251     val allOntClassIRIsZ = ZIO
252       .foreach(querySolutions) { qs =>
253         ZIO.foreach(qs.varNames.asScala.filter(_.endsWith("_type")).to(Iterable)) { typeVar =>
254           ZIO.effect(IRI(qs.getResource(typeVar).getURI)).mapError { e =>
255             new Exception(s"Value of _type variable $typeVar is not a URI", e)
256           }
257         }
258       }
259       .map(_.flatten)
260     val allQueryNodeIDs = queryGraph.nodes.keySet
261     for {
262       allOntClassIRIs <- allOntClassIRIsZ
263       nodeDetails <- getTRAPINodeDetails(allOntClassIRIs)
264       termToLabelAndTypes = nodeDetails.groupBy(_.term).map { case (term, termsAndTypes) =>
265         val (labels, biolinkTypes) = termsAndTypes.map(t => t.label -> t.biolinkType).unzip
266         term -> (labels.flatten.headOption, biolinkTypes)
267       }
268       trapiNodes <- ZIO.foreach(querySolutions) { querySolution =>
269         for {
270           nodes <- ZIO.foreach(allQueryNodeIDs) { queryNodeID =>
271             for {
272               nodeIRI <- ZIO
273                 .effect(querySolution.getResource(s"${queryNodeID}_type").getURI)
274                 .orElseFail(new Exception(s"Missing node IRI: $queryNodeID"))
275               labelAndTypes = termToLabelAndTypes.getOrElse(IRI(nodeIRI), (None, List(BiolinkNamedThing)))
276               (labelOpt, biolinkTypes) = labelAndTypes
277               biolinkTypesSet = biolinkTypes.to(Set)
278               nodeBiolinkTypes = bionlinkClasses.filter(c => biolinkTypesSet(c.iri))
279             } yield IRI(nodeIRI) -> TRAPINode(labelOpt, Some(nodeBiolinkTypes), None)
280           }
281         } yield nodes.toList
282       }
283     } yield trapiNodes.flatten.toMap
284   }
285 
286   def getTRAPINodeDetailsQueryText(nodeIdList: List[IRI]): QueryText = {
287     // requiring biolinkType makes some terms not be found when these results are used elsewhere - must be handled there
288     val nodeIds = nodeIdList.map(n => sparql" $n ").fold(sparql"")(_ + _)
289     sparql"""SELECT ?term ?biolinkType (MIN(?term_label) AS ?label)
290          WHERE {
291            VALUES ?term { $nodeIds }
292            ?term $RDFSSubClassOf ?biolinkType .
293            ?biolinkType $BiolinkMLIsA* ${BiolinkNamedThing.iri} .
294            OPTIONAL { ?term $RDFSLabel ?term_label }
295          }
296          GROUP BY ?term ?biolinkType"""
297   }
298 
299   def getTRAPINodeDetails(nodeIdList: List[IRI]): RIO[ZConfig[AppConfig] with HttpClient, List[TermWithLabelAndBiolinkType]] =
300     for {
301       queryText <- Task.effect(getTRAPINodeDetailsQueryText(nodeIdList))
302       termsAndBiolinkTypes <- SPARQLQueryExecutor.runSelectQueryAs[TermWithLabelAndBiolinkType](queryText.toQuery)
303     } yield termsAndBiolinkTypes

305   def getTRAPINodeBindings(queryGraph: TRAPIQueryGraph,
306                            querySolution: QuerySolution): ZIO[Any, Throwable, Map[String, List[TRAPINodeBinding]]] =
307     for {
308       nodeMap <- Task.effect(queryGraph.nodes.map(n => (n._1, querySolution.get(s"${n._1}_type").toString)))
309       nodeBindings <- ZIO.foreach(queryGraph.nodes) { (k, v) =>
310         for {
311           nodeIRI <- ZIO.fromOption(nodeMap.get(k)).orElseFail(new Exception(s"Missing node IRI: $k"))
312         } yield k -> List(TRAPINodeBinding(IRI(nodeIRI)))
313       }
314     } yield nodeBindings

316   def getTRAPIEdgeBindingsMany(queryGraph: TRAPIQueryGraph,
317                                querySolutions: List[QuerySolution],
318                                relationsMap: Map[IRI, (Option[String], IRI)])
319     : ZIO[ZConfig[AppConfig] with HttpClient with Has[BiolinkData], Throwable, Map[QuerySolution, Map[String, List[TRAPIEdgeBinding]]]] =
320     for {
321       biolinkData <- biolinkData
322       querySolutionsToEdgeBindings <- ZIO.foreach(querySolutions) { querySolution =>
323         for {
324           edgeBindings <- ZIO.foreach(queryGraph.edges) { (queryEdgeID, queryEdge) =>
325             for {
326               sourceType <- Task.effect(querySolution.get(s"${queryEdge.subject}_type").toString)
327               targetType <- Task.effect(querySolution.get(s"${queryEdge.`object`}_type").toString)
328               relation = querySolution.getResource(queryEdgeID).getURI
329               relationIRI = IRI(relation)
330               relationLabelAndBiolinkPredicate <- ZIO
331                 .fromOption(relationsMap.get(relationIRI))
332                 .orElseFail(new Exception("Unexpected edge relation"))
333               (relationLabelOpt, biolinkPredicateIRI) = relationLabelAndBiolinkPredicate
334               blPred = biolinkData.predicates.find(a => a.iri == biolinkPredicateIRI)
335               trapiEdgeKey = getTRAPIEdgeKey(sourceType, blPred, targetType)
336               trapiEdgeBinding = List(TRAPIEdgeBinding(trapiEdgeKey))
337             } yield queryEdgeID -> trapiEdgeBinding
338           }
339         } yield querySolution -> edgeBindings
340       }
341     } yield querySolutionsToEdgeBindings.toMap

343   def getProvenanceQueryText(edges: Set[Triple]): QueryText = {
344     val values = edges.map(e => sparql"( ${e.subj} ${e.pred} ${e.obj} )").fold(sparql"")(_ + _)
345     sparql"""SELECT ?s ?p ?o ?g ?other
346         WHERE {
347           VALUES (?s ?p ?o) { $values }
348           GRAPH ?g { ?s ?p ?o }
349           OPTIONAL { ?g $ProvWasDerivedFrom ?other . }
350         }"""
351   }
352 
353   def getProvenance(edges: Set[Triple]): ZIO[ZConfig[AppConfig] with HttpClient, Throwable, Map[TripleString, String]] =
354     for {
355       queryText <- Task.effect(getProvenanceQueryText(edges))
356       querySolutions <- SPARQLQueryExecutor.runSelectQuery(queryText.toQuery)
357       triplesToGraphs <- ZIO.foreach(querySolutions) { solution =>
358         Task.effect {
359           val graph = if (solution.contains("other")) solution.getResource("other").getURI else solution.getResource("g").getURI
360           val triple = TripleString(solution.getResource("s").getURI, solution.getResource("p").getURI, solution.getResource("o").getURI)
361           triple -> graph
362         }
363       }
364     } yield triplesToGraphs.toMap

366   def getCAMStuffQueryText(prov: IRI): QueryText =
367     sparql"""SELECT DISTINCT (?s_type AS ?subj) (?p AS ?pred) (?o_type AS ?obj)
368          WHERE { GRAPH $prov {
369              ?s ?p ?o .
370              ?s $RDFType $OWLNamedIndividual .
371              ?o $RDFType $OWLNamedIndividual .
372            }
373          ?o $SesameDirectType ?o_type .
374          ?s $SesameDirectType ?s_type .
375          FILTER(isIRI(?o_type))
376          FILTER(isIRI(?s_type))
377        }"""
378 
379   def getCAMStuff(prov: IRI): RIO[ZConfig[AppConfig] with HttpClient, List[Triple]] =
380     for {
381       queryText <- Task.effect(getCAMStuffQueryText(prov))
382       triples <- SPARQLQueryExecutor.runSelectQueryAs[Triple](queryText.toQuery)
383     } yield triples

385   def getExtraKGNodes(camNodes: Set[IRI],
386                       slotStuffNodeDetails: List[TermWithLabelAndBiolinkType],
387                       biolinkData: BiolinkData): Map[IRI, TRAPINode] = {
388     val termToLabelAndTypes = slotStuffNodeDetails.groupBy(_.term).map { case (term, termsAndTypes) =>
389       val (labels, biolinkTypes) = termsAndTypes.map(t => t.label -> t.biolinkType).unzip
390       term -> (labels.flatten.headOption, biolinkTypes)
391     }
392     val nodeMap = camNodes.map { node =>
393       val (labelOpt, biolinkTypes) = termToLabelAndTypes.getOrElse(node, (None, List(BiolinkNamedThing)))
394       val biolinkTypesSet = biolinkTypes.to(Set)
395       val classes = biolinkData.classes.filter(c => biolinkTypesSet(c.iri))
396       node -> TRAPINode(labelOpt, Some(classes), None)
397     }.toMap
398     nodeMap
399   }
400 
401   def mapRelationsToLabelAndBiolink(relations: Set[IRI]): RIO[ZConfig[AppConfig] with HttpClient, Map[IRI, (Option[String], IRI)]] = {
402     final case class RelationInfo(relation: IRI, biolinkSlot: IRI, label: Option[String])
403     val queryText = sparql"""
404          SELECT DISTINCT ?relation ?biolinkSlot ?label
405          WHERE {
406            VALUES ?relation { ${relations.asValues} }
407            ?relation $SlotMapping ?biolinkSlot .
408            ?biolinkSlot a $BiolinkMLSlotDefinition .
409            OPTIONAL { ?relation $RDFSLabel ?label . }
410            FILTER NOT EXISTS {
411              ?relation $SlotMapping ?other .
412              ?other $BiolinkMLIsA+/$BiolinkMLMixins* ?biolinkSlot .
413            }
414          }"""
415     SPARQLQueryExecutor.runSelectQueryAs[RelationInfo](queryText.toQuery).map { res =>
416       res.groupMap(_.relation)(info => (info.label, info.biolinkSlot)).map { case (relationIRI, infos) => relationIRI -> infos.head }
417     }
418   }
419 
420   def mapQueryBiolinkPredicatesToRelations(
421     predicates: Set[BiolinkPredicate]): RIO[ZConfig[AppConfig] with HttpClient with Has[SPARQLCache], Map[BiolinkPredicate, Set[IRI]]] = {
422     final case class Predicate(biolinkPredicate: BiolinkPredicate, predicate: IRI)
423     val queryText = sparql"""
424         SELECT DISTINCT ?biolinkPredicate ?predicate WHERE {
425           VALUES ?biolinkPredicate { ${predicates.asValues} }
426           ?predicate $SlotMapping ?biolinkPredicate .
427           FILTER EXISTS { ?s ?predicate ?o }
428           <http://www.bigdata.com/queryHints#Query> <http://www.bigdata.com/queryHints#filterExists> "SubQueryLimitOne"
429         }"""
430     for {
431       predicates <- SPARQLQueryExecutor.runSelectQueryWithCacheAs[Predicate](queryText.toQuery)
432     } yield predicates.to(Set).groupMap(_.biolinkPredicate)(_.predicate)
433   }
